***helm.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:helm.html>helm</a> (4399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:helm.html>helm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*helmaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:helm.html>helm</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:helm.html>Helm</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:helm.html>Helm</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hjelm</i>.
</p>

***helpen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a> (206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">helpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*helpaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to help
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a></b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Whom may I <b>help</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to provide, to supply [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span>(with)</span></span>]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedankt.html>Bedankt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:truitje.html>truitje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geholpen.html>geholpen</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>Thanks</a> for <b>getting</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> that sweater!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get hooked, to cause (someone) to be very keen (on), addicted or depended [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span>(to)</span></span>]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> vriendengroup <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geholpen.html>geholpen</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That circle of friends <b>got</b> her <b>addicted</b> to alcohol.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hels.html>hels</a> (21920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hels.html>hels</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hels.html>helser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hels.html>hels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">helst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hellish</span>, in or related to hell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilder.html>schilder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorliefde.html>voorliefde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:helse.html>helse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:taferelen.html>taferelen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This painter <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a predilection for <a href = vnd.unilang:scenes.html>scenes</a> <b>featuring hell</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>diabolically horrible, gruesome</li>
<li>devilishly extreme, intense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opeens.html>Opeens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klonk.html>klonk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hels.html>hels</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabaal.html>kabaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanuit.html>vanuit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> café. <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nam.html>nam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Suddenly an <b>enormous</b> uproar sounded from the café. So I supposed that the <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> still made it in time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chemically aggressive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:helse.html>helse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:steen.html>steen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>hellish stone</b> (i.e. silver nitrate).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hemde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hemede</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hemithi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hamiþiją</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemd.html>Hemd</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">העמד</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemd.html>hemd</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***hemelbed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemelbed.html>hemelbed</a> (82849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cover, canopy; heaven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelbed.html>hemelbed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelbedden.html>hemelbedden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelbed.html>hemelbedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***hemelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemelen.html>hemelen</a> (10234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêmelen</i>. The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimelijk.html>heimelijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">secret</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and in early modern Dutch it still meant "to clean up, to tidy". Semantic influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heaven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> likely shifted its meaning from this towards "to make nice, to make beautiful" and then to the current sense.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelen.html>hemelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hide, to remove</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fix, to repair</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelen.html>hemelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>, with the implication of going to heaven</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelen.html>hemelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hemelen.html>hemelen</a></b>  <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>

***hen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> (323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*himaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>them <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">object pronoun</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>See the usage note at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> for <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a> on use.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">henne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:henna.html>henna</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanjō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂n-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hennen.html>hennen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">hennetje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haan.html>haan</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></a>, female chicken; female of a related species.</li>
<li>A female of the species of <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> brooding on the ground.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> 'bird', colloquial term for a human female</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hannep</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hennep.html>hennep</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hanap</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*henip</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanapiz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hanf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hemp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamp.html>hamp</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*heribergo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bergô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shelter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herder.html>herder</a> (7004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:herder.html>herder</a></i>, earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">herde</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*herdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herd</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-e</i>; the <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> replaced <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-e</i> when the latter fell in disuse as signifying agency.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herder.html>herder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herders.html>herders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herdertje.html>herdertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herderin.html>herderin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>herdsman, herd, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:herder.html>herder</a></span></li>
<li>sheepdog
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herdershond.html>herdershond</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">her-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herdrukken.html>herdrukken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reprint</li></ol>

***herfst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a> (5103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hervist</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harbistaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kerp-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Herbst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Harvst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hjerst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">harvest</i>; further with Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carpere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pick, to pluck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καρπός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karpós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fruit, harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The original meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> “harvest time”, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seen in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">herfstmaand</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>autumn, fall</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:najaar.html>najaar</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:jaargetijde.html>jaargetijde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zomer.html>zomer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> winter

***herinneren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a> (988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th century, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">erinnern</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">erinnern</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remind, prompt

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ditransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, remind oneself

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herinnering.html>herinnering</a> (2957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinnering.html>herinnering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinneringen.html>herinneringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinnering.html>herinneringetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A memory, something that one remembers.</li>
<li>The act of remembering.</li>
<li>A reminder, something that reminds one about something.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>souvenir</a>, a keepsake.</li></ol>
